<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">недо-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nedo-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:любить.html>люби́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ljubítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ивать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ivatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to have no special liking/sympathy <i>(for)</i>, to have a dislike <i>(for)</i>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:недомогание.html>недомога́ние</a> (14425)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">недомога́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nedomogátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ние</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ánije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:недомогание.html>недомога́ние</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nedomogánije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:недомогание.html>недомога́ния</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:недомогание.html>недомога́ния</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:недомогание.html>недомога́ний</a></b>)

<ol><li>malaise, lethargy, malady</li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:до.html>до</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:мо.html>мо</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:га.html>га́</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:ни.html>ни</a><span class="hyph-dot" style="color:red;">·</span>е</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:существительное.html>Существи́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:неодушевленный.html>неодушевлённое</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:средний.html>сре́дний</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:род.html>род</a>, 2-е <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ние</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> 7a  <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 4c(7).
Соответствуюший <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:недооценивать.html>недооце́нивать</a>.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:приставка.html>Приста́вки</a>: <b>не-до-о-</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>ко́рень</a>: <b>-цен-</b>; суффикс: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:соорудить.html>-и</a></b>; глагольное <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ть</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.
</p>
<h4><span id=".D0.97.D0.BD.D0.B0.D1.87.D0.B5.D0.BD.D0.B8.D0.B5"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Значение"><a href = vnd.unilang:значение.html>Значе́ние</a></span></h4>
<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:оценить.html>оцени́ть</a> кого-либо, что-либо <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:полный.html>по́лной</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мера.html>ме́ре</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:недостаточно.html>недоста́точно</a> <span class="example-fullblock"><br><span class="example-block" style="color:darkgreen">Рожественский <a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>был</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:слишком.html>сли́шком</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:самоуверенный.html>самоуве́рен</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:считать.html>счита́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>себя́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:гениальный.html>гениа́льным</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:но.html>но</a> <span class="example-select" style="background-color: EDF0FF; font-weight: bold;"><a href = vnd.unilang:недооценить.html>недооцени́л</a></span> <a href = vnd.unilang:способность.html>спосо́бностей</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:свое.html>своего́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:противник.html>проти́вника</a>. <span class="example-details" style="font-size:smaller;"> <i><a href="https://ru.wikipedia.org/wiki/%D0%9D%D0%BE%D0%B2%D0%B8%D0%BA%D0%BE%D0%B2-%D0%9F%D1%80%D0%B8%D0%B1%D0%BE%D0%B9,_%D0%90%D0%BB%D0%B5%D0%BA%D1%81%D0%B5%D0%B9_%D0%A1%D0%B8%D0%BB%D1%8B%D1%87" class="extiw" title="w:Новиков-Прибой, Алексей Силыч"><a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>С</a>. <p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:недоразумение.html>недоразуме́ние</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nedorazuménije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:недоразумение.html>недоразуме́ния</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:недоразумение.html>недоразуме́ния</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:недоразумение.html>недоразуме́ний</a></b>)

***недоставать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:недоставать.html>недостава́ть</a> (13726)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:недопить.html>не-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ne-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:доставать.html>достава́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">dostavátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:недоставать.html>недостава́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nedostavátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">недоста́ть</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to lack, to be needed
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>чего́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>вам</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:недоставать.html>недостаёт</a></b>?</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">čevó vam <b>nedostajót</b>?</i> ― <span class="e-translation">what are you short of?; what are you lacking?</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>ему́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:недоставать.html>недостаёт</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:деньги.html>де́нег</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">jemú <b>nedostajót</b> déneg</i> ― <span class="e-translation">he is short of money</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>нам</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:недоставать.html>недостаёт</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:работник.html>рабо́тников</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">nam <b>nedostajót</b> rabótnikov</i> ― <span class="e-translation">we lack workers; we are short of workers</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>ему́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:недоставать.html>недостаёт</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:слово.html>сло́в</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:чтобы.html>что́бы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:выразить.html>вы́разить</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">jemú <b>nedostajót</b> slov, štóby výrazitʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">he cannot find words to express</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>ему́</a> <b>недоста́нет</b> <a href = vnd.unilang:сила.html>си́л</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">jemú <b>nedostánet</b> sil</i> ― <span class="e-translation">his strength will not suffice him; he will not have sufficient strength</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́того</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:еще.html>ещё</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:недоставать.html>недостава́ло</a></b>!</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">étovo ješčó <b>nedostaválo</b>!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">that's all we needed</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to miss
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>нам</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:очень.html>о́чень</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:недоставать.html>недостава́ло</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>вас</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">nam óčenʹ <b>nedostaválo</b> vas</i> ― <span class="e-translation">we missed you very much; we missed you badly</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">недоста́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nedostátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ок</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ok</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:недостаток.html>недоста́ток</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nedostátok</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:недостаток.html>недоста́тка</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:недостаток.html>недоста́тки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:недостаток.html>недоста́тков</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>lack, deficiency, deficit, shortage</li>
<li>defect, drawback, flaw</li></ol>
